compactable blocks in the provided directory.\\n222: func (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\\n223: \\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\\n224: \\tif err != nil {\\n225: \\t\\treturn \\n254: \\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\\n255: \\tif len(res) > 0 {\\n256: \\t\\treturn res, nil\\n257: \\t}\\n258: \\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\\n259: \\t// We do having to care about data overlap.\\n261: \\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\\n262: \\n263: \\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\\n264: \\t\\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\\n265: \\t}\\n266: \\tif len(res) > \\n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\\n292: \\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\\n293: \\t\\treturn nil\\n294: \\t}\\n295: \\n296: \\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\\n297: \\n298: \\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\\n299: \\t\\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\\n300: \\t\\tif len(parts) == 0 {\\n301: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n302: \\t\\t}\\n303: \\n304: \\tOuter:\\n305: \\t\\tfor _, p := range parts {\\n306: \\t\\t\\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\\n307: \\t\\t\\tfor _, dm := range p {\\n308: \\t\\t\\t\\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\\n309: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue Outer\\n310: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n311: \\t\\t\\t}\\n312: \\n313: \\t\\t\\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\\n314: \\t\\t\\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\\n315: \\t\\t\\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\\n316: \\t\\t\\t// or is before the most recent block.\\n317: \\t\\t\\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\\n318: \\t\\t\\t// size still fits in the range.\\n319: \\t\\t\\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\\n320: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn p\\n321: \\t\\t\\t}\\n322: \\t\\t}\\n323: \\t}\\n324: \\n325: \\treturn nil\\n326: }\\n327: \\n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\\n331: \\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\\n332: \\t\\treturn nil\\n333: \\t}\\n334: \\tif len(ds) < 2 {\\n335: \\t\\treturn nil\\n336: \\t}\\n337: \\tvar overlappingDirs []string\\n338: \\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\\n339: \\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\\n340: \\t\\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\\n341: \\t\\t\\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\\n342: \\t\\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\\n343: \\t\\t\\t}\\n344: \\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\\n345: \\t\\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\\n346: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n347: \\t\\t}\\n348: \\t\\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\\n349: \\t\\t\\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\\n350: \\t\\t}\\n351: \\t}\\n352: \\treturn overlappingDirs\\n353: }\\n354: \\n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\\n356: //\\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\\n360: \\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\\n361: \\n362: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\\n363: \\t\\tvar (\\n364: \\t\\t\\tgroup []dirMeta\\n365: \\t\\t\\tt0    int64\\n366: \\t\\t\\tm     = ds[i].meta\\n367: \\t\\t)\\n368: \\t\\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\\n369: \\t\\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\\n370: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\\n371: \\t\\t} else {\\n372: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\\n373: \\t\\t}\\n374: \\t\\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\\n375: \\t\\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\\n376: \\t\\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n377: \\t\\t\\ti++\\n378: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n379: \\t\\t}\\n380: \\n381: \\t\\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\\n382: \\t\\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\\n383: \\t\\t\\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\\n384: \\t\\t\\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n385: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n386: \\t\\t\\t}\\n387: \\t\\t\\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\\n388: \\t\\t}\\n389: \\n390: \\t\\tif len(group) > 0 {\\n391: \\t\\t\\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\\n392: \\t\\t}\\n393: \\t}\\n394: \\n395: \\treturn splitDirs\\n396: }\\n397: \\n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. \\n254: \\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\\n255: \\tif len(res) > 0 {\\n256: \\t\\treturn res, nil\\n257: \\t}\\n258: \\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\\n259: \\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\\n260: \\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\\n261: \\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\\n262: \\n263: \\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\\n264: \\t\\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\\n265: \\t}\\n266: \\tif len(res) > 0 {\\n267: \\t\\treturn res, nil\\n268: \\t}\\n269: \\n270: \\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\\n271: \\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\\n272: \\t\\tmeta := dms[i].meta\\n273: \\t\\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\\n274: \\t\\t\\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\\n275: \\t\\t\\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\\n276: \\t\\t\\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\\n277: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\\n278: \\t\\t\\t}\\n279: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n280: \\t\\t}\\n281: \\t\\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\\n282: \\t\\t\\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\\n283: \\t\\t}\\n284: \\t}\\n285: \\n286: \\treturn nil, nil\\n287: }\\n288: \\n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\\n292: \\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\\n293: \\t\\treturn nil\\n294: \\t}\\n295: \\n296: \\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\\n297: \\n298: \\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\\n299: \\t\\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\\n300: \\t\\tif len(parts) == 0 {\\n301: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n302: \\t\\t}\\n303: \\n304: \\tOuter:\\n305: \\t\\tfor _, p := range parts {\\n306: \\t\\t\\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\\n307: \\t\\t\\tfor _, dm := range p {\\n308: \\t\\t\\t\\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\\n309: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue Outer\\n310: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n311: \\t\\t\\t}\\n312: \\n313: \\t\\t\\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\\n314: \\t\\t\\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\\n315: \\t\\t\\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\\n316: \\t\\t\\t// or is before the most recent block.\\n317: \\t\\t\\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\\n318: \\t\\t\\t// size still fits in the range.\\n319: \\t\\t\\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\\n320: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn p\\n321: \\t\\t\\t}\\n322: \\t\\t}\\n323: \\t}\\n324: \\n325: \\treturn nil\\n326: }\\n327: \\n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\\n331: \\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\\n332: \\t\\treturn nil\\n333: \\t}\\n334: \\tif len(ds) < 2 {\\n335: \\t\\treturn nil\\n336: \\t}\\n337: \\tvar overlappingDirs []string\\n338: \\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\\n339: \\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\\n340: \\t\\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\\n341: \\t\\t\\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\\n342: \\t\\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\\n343: \\t\\t\\t}\\n344: \\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\\n345: \\t\\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\\n346: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n347: \\t\\t}\\n348: \\t\\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\\n349: \\t\\t\\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\\n350: \\t\\t}\\n351: \\t}\\n352: \\treturn overlappingDirs\\n353: }\\n354: \\n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\\n356: //\\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\\n360: \\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\\n361: \\n362: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\\n363: \\t\\tvar (\\n364: \\t\\t\\tgroup []dirMeta\\n365: \\t\\t\\tt0    int64\\n366: \\t\\t\\tm     = ds[i].meta\\n367: \\t\\t)\\n368: \\t\\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\\n369: \\t\\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\\n370: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\\n371: \\t\\t} else {\\n372: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\\n373: \\t\\t}\\n374: \\t\\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\\n375: \\t\\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\\n376: \\t\\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n377: \\t\\t\\ti++\\n378: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n379: \\t\\t}\\n380: \\n381: \\t\\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\\n382: \\t\\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\\n383: \\t\\t\\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\\n384: \\t\\t\\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n385: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n386: \\t\\t\\t}\\n387: \\t\\t\\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\\n388: \\t\\t}\\n389: \\n390: \\t\\tif len(group) > 0 {\\n391: \\t\\t\\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\\n392: \\t\\t}\\n393: \\t}\\n394: \\n395: \\treturn splitDirs\\n396: }\\n397: \\n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\\n400: func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\\n401: \\tres := &BlockMeta{\\n402: \\t\\tULID: uid,\\n403: \\t\\t}\\n422: \\t\\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\\n423: \\t\\t\\tULID:    b.ULID,\\n424: \\t\\t\\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\\n425: \\t\\t\\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\\n426: c.plan(dms)\n240: }\n241: \n242: func (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n243: \tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n244: \t\tswitch {\n245: \t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n246: \t\t\treturn -1\n247: \t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n248: \t\t\treturn 1\n249: \t\tdefault:\n250: \t\t\treturn 0\n251: \t\t}\n252: \t})\n253: \n254: \tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n255: \tif len(res) > 0 {\n256: \t\treturn res, nil\n257: \t}\n258: \t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n259: \t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n260: \t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n261: \tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n262: \n263: \tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n264: \t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n265: \t}\n266: \tif len(res) > 0 {\n267: \t\treturn res, nil\n268: \t}\n269: \n270: \t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n271: \tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n272: \t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n273: \t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n274: \t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n275: \t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n276: \t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n277: \t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n278: \t\t\t}\n279: \t\t\tbreak\n280: \t\t}\n281: \t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n282: \t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n283: \t\t}\n284: \t}\n285: \n286: \treturn nil, nil\n287: }\n288: \n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n292: \tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n293: \t\treturn nil\n294: \t}\n295: \n296: \thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n297: \n298: \tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n299: \t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n300: \t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n301: \t\t\tcontinue\n302: \t\t}\n303: \n304: \tOuter:\n305: \t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n306: \t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n307: \t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n308: \t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n309: \t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n310: \t\t\t\t}\n311: \t\t\t}\n312: \n313: \t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n314: \t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n315: \t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n316: \t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n317: \t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n318: \t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n319: \t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n320: \t\t\t\treturn p\n321: \t\t\t}\n322: \t\t}\n323: \t}\n324: \n325: \treturn nil\n326: }\n327: \n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n331: \tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n332: \t\treturn nil\n333: \t}\n334: \tif len(ds) < 2 {\n335: \t\treturn nil\n336: \t}\n337: \tvar overlappingDirs []string\n338: \tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n339: \tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n340: \t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n341: \t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n342: \t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n343: \t\t\t}\n344: \t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n345: \t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n346: \t\t\tbreak\n347: \t\t}\n348: \t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n349: \t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n350: \t\t}\n351: \t}\n352: \treturn overlappingDirs\n353: }\n354: \n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n356: //\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n360: \tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n361: \n362: \tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n363: \t\tvar (\n364: \t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n365: \t\t\tt0    int64\n366: \t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n367: \t\t)\n368: \t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n369: \t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n370: \t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n371: \t\t} else {\n372: \t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n373: \t\t}\n374: \t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n375: \t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n376: \t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n377: \t\t\ti++\n378: \t\t\tcontinue\n379: \t\t}\n380: \n381: \t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n382: \t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n383: \t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n384: \t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n385: \t\t\t\tbreak\n386: \t\t\t}\n387: \t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n388: \t\t}\n389: \n390: \t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n391: \t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n392: \t\t}\n393: \t}\n394: \n395: \treturn splitDirs\n396: }\n397: \n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n400: func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n401: \tres := &BlockMeta{\n402: \t\tULID: uid,\n403: type Options struct {\\n92: \\t// Segments (wal files) max size.\\n93: \\t// WALSegmentSize = 0, segment size is default size.\\n94: \\t// WALSegmentSize > 0, segment size is WALSegmentSize.\\n95: \\t// WALSegmentSize < 0, wal is disabled.\\n96: \\tWALSegmentSize int\\n97: \\n98: \\t// MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize is the max size of block chunk segment files.\\n99: \\t// MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize = \\tRetentionDuration int64\\n107: \\n108: \\t// Maximum number of bytes in blocks to be retained.\\n109: \\t// 0 or less means disabled.\\n110: \\t// NOTE: For proper storage calculations need to consider\\n111: \\t// the size of the WAL folder which is not added when calculating\\n112: \\t// the current size of the database.\\n113: \\tMaxBytes int64\\n114: \\n115: \\t// NoLockfile disables int\\n124: \\n125: \\t// StripeSize is the size in entries of the series hash map. Reducing the size will save memory but impact performance.\\n126: \\tStripeSize int\\n127: \\n128: \\t// The timestamp range of head blocks after which they get persisted.\\n129: \\t// It's the minimum duration of any persisted block.\\n130: \\t// Unit agnostic as long as unit is consistent with RetentionDuration and MaxBlockDuration.\\n131: \\t// Typically it is in milliseconds.\\n132: \\tMinBlockDuration int64\\n133: \\n134: \\t// The maximum timestamp range of compacted blocks.\\n135: \\t// Unit agnostic as long as unit is consistent with MinBlockDuration and RetentionDuration.\\n136: \\t// Typically it is in milliseconds.\\n137: \\tMaxBlockDuration int64\\n138: \\n139: \\t// HeadChunksWriteBufferSize configures the write buffer size used by the head chunks mapper.\\n140: \\tHeadChunksWriteBufferSize int\\n141: \\n142: \\t// HeadChunksWriteQueueSize configures the size of the chunk write queue used in the head chunks mapper.\\n143: \\tHeadChunksWriteQueueSize int\\n144: \\n145: \\t// SamplesPerChunk configures the target number of samples per chunk.\\n146: \\tSamplesPerChunk int\\n147: \\n148: \\t// SeriesLifecycleCallback specifies a list of callbacks that will be called during a lifecycle of a series.\\n149: \\t// It is always a no-op in Prometheus and mainly meant for external users who import TSDB.\\n150: \\tSeriesLifecycleCallback SeriesLifecycleCallback\\n151: \\n152: \\t// BlocksToDelete is a function which returns the blocks which can be deleted.\\n153: \\t// It is always the default time and size based retention in Prometheus and\\n154: \\t// mainly meant for external users who import TSDB.\\n155: \\tBlocksToDelete BlocksToDeleteFunc\\n156: \\n157: \\t// Enables the in memory exemplar storage.\\n158: \\tEnableExemplarStorage bool\\n159: \\n160: \\t// Enables the snapshot of in-memory chunks on shutdown. Overview\n\n### What is Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time-series blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. It serves three primary purposes:\n\n1. **Space Efficiency**: Consolidates data from smaller 2-hour blocks into larger blocks (up to 31 days or 10% of retention), reducing metadata overhead\n2. **Query Performance**: Fewer blocks to scan during queries, reducing I/O and improving query speed\n3. **Tombstone Cleanup**: Removes series marked for deletion (via tombstones), recovering disk space\n\n### Block Structure\n\nPrometheus stores time-series data in a hierarchical block structure with exponential block durations:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: In-memory head block, ~2 hours of data\n- **Level 1-10**: Persisted blocks with exponentially increasing durations\n  - Each level is ~3x larger than the previous level\n  - Example: 2h → 6h → 18h → 54h → ... → 31 days\n  - Blocks containing tombstones (>5% deleted series) are also compacted\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered through two mechanisms:\n\n| Trigger Type | Frequency | Condition |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Head Block Compaction** | On append commit | `head.compactable()` returns true when head block age > `chunkRange / 2` |\n| **Scheduled Compaction** | Every 1 minute | Regular background loop in `db.run()` checks for blocks ready to compact |\n| **Block Compaction** | On-demand | Multiple level-0/1 blocks fitting within a time range are merged upward |\n\n**Code References:**\n- Head compaction trigger: `dbAppender.Commit()` (tsdb/db.go:1115-1127)\n- Scheduled trigger: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compaction logic: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Critical Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Execution Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Increasing | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions scheduled | Increasing regularly | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compaction attempts | Should be 0 or growing slowly | `increase(...[1h]) > 5` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to auto-compact disabled | Stable or low | `rate(...[5m]) > 0` indicates disabled compaction |\n\n#### Performance Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` (histogram) | Histogram | Time to complete compaction | p99 < block_duration | p99 > `chunkRange` (2h default) suggests falling behind |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` (gauge) | Gauge | Block being written (1=yes, 0=no) | 0 (not perpetually writing) | Stuck at 1 for >10 minutes |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases as blocks overlap | Rapid increase suggests ingestion delays |\n\n#### Block & Storage Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of persistent blocks in memory | Increases then stable | Continuously increasing suggests compaction not running |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` | Gauge | Memory for symbol tables across blocks | Stable/growing slowly | Rapid growth with `blocks_loaded` suggests memory leak |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Disk space used by blocks | Stable near `retention_limit_bytes` | Exceeds `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max retention size | Set once | Mismatch with actual disk usage |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (time-based) | Stable or increasing | Increasing rapidly suggests retention misconfiguration |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (size-based) | Stable or slow increase | Increasing suggests `MaxBytes` limit being hit |\n\n#### WAL/Checkpointing Metrics\n\n| Metric | Meaning | Healthy | Watch For |\n|--------|---------|---------|-----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total` | WAL corruption count | 0 or stable | Increasing indicates disk issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_truncate_duration_seconds` | WAL truncation time | < 1 second | > 5 seconds suggests slow disk I/O |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Indicators\n\nA healthy Prometheus instance should exhibit:\n\n```\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total continuously increasing\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total stable (not growing)\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 < 2 hours (default block range)\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded stable after reaching equilibrium\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 0 (not perpetually writing)\n✓ No increase in prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total\n```\n\n### Stuck Compaction Indicators\n\nCompaction is stuck if:\n\n```\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 1 for >10 minutes\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 > 2× block_duration\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded continuously increasing\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total increasing but compactions_failed_total also increasing\n✗ Logs show \"compaction failed\" repeatedly\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` exceeds available disk space\n- Compaction fails with I/O errors\n- Prometheus logs: `error: write block: no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New samples may be rejected; WAL may grow unbounded\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Retention period/MaxBytes configured too large for available disk\n- Compaction not running (blocks accumulate uncompacted)\n- Retention deletion running slower than ingestion\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage and free space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect block count and sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n3. Check Prometheus metrics:\n   ```\n   prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes (current size)\n   prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes (configured limit)\n   prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded (number of blocks)\n   ```\n\n4. Review Prometheus logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compaction\\|disk\\|space\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Action (Buy Time)**\n   - Stop ingestion temporarily (pause scrape jobs) if possible\n   - Disable auto-compaction to free CPU for deletion:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n2. **Free Disk Space (Choose One)**\n\n   **Option A: Reduce Retention**\n   - Edit `prometheus.yml`, reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `storage.tsdb.retention.size`\n   - Restart Prometheus\n   - Blocks older than new retention are deleted on next compaction\n\n   **Option B: Manual Block Deletion**\n   - **Backup first**: `tar czf prometheus-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/blocks/`\n   - List blocks by age:\n     ```bash\n     promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable\n     ```\n   - Manually delete oldest blocks (oldest ULID = earliest blocks):\n     ```bash\n     rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/01ARZ3NHH000000000 # Replace ULID\n     ```\n   - Reload Prometheus via admin API:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n   **Option C: Extend Disk (Preferred Long-term)**\n   - Add more disk capacity\n   - Mount at same path or symlink\n\n3. **Restart Compaction**\n   ```bash\n   # Enable auto-compaction (if disabled)\n   curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/clean_tombstones\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify Recovery**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` decreasing\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` stops increasing\n   - Re-enable scrape jobs\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction error handling: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Retention deletion: `db.reloadBlocks()` (tsdb/db.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 10 minutes (stuck at \"writing block\")\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` histogram not updating\n- Prometheus CPU usage high, disk I/O high, but no new blocks created\n- Logs show \"compact blocks\" but no completion\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Out-of-Memory (OOM) killing compaction process** (see Failure Mode 4)\n- **Disk I/O bottleneck** (slow SSDs, network storage, VM I/O throttling)\n- **Lock contention** (cmtx held, blocking other operations)\n- **Query load during compaction** interfering with I/O scheduling\n- **WAL replay still running** in background, holding file locks\n- **Context cancelled** (Prometheus shutting down, compaction context timed out)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check compaction duration trend:\n   ```\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_sum[5m]) / rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_count[5m])\n   ```\n   Should complete in < 2 hours (default block duration)\n\n2. Check if block is being written:\n   ```bash\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n   ```\n   If true for > 10 min, compaction is stuck.\n\n3. Check for hanging processes:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus  # Check CPU/memory\n   lsof /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path | head -20  # Check open files\n   ```\n\n4. Check disk I/O:\n   ```bash\n   iostat -x 1 10  # Check %utilization, await time\n   iotop -o        # Monitor top I/O processes\n   ```\n\n5. Review recent logs:\n   ```bash\n   tail -100 prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|error\\|warn\"\n   ```\n\n6. Check WAL replay status:\n   ```\n   # Look for \"msg\"=\"WAL read\" or \"OOO replay\" in logs\n   grep -i \"wal read\\|ooo.*replay\" prometheus.log | tail -10\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Determine Root Cause** (from diagnostics above)\n\n2. **If OOM (see Failure Mode 4)**\n   - Increase memory limit\n   - Reduce `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size` (default 512MB)\n   - Reduce ingestion rate\n\n3. **If Disk I/O Bottleneck**\n   - Reduce query concurrency (scale down dashboards/alerts)\n   - Move TSDB to faster storage (SSD preferred)\n   - For network storage: check latency, throughput, cache settings\n\n4. **If Compaction Truly Stuck (20+ minutes)**\n   - Stop Prometheus gracefully:\n     ```bash\n     kill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n     # Wait up to 5 minutes for graceful shutdown\n     sleep 300\n     kill -9 <prometheus-pid>  # Force if needed\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus:\n     ```bash\n     systemctl restart prometheus\n     # OR\n     /path/to/prometheus --config.file=prometheus.yml\n     ```\n   - Prometheus will replay WAL and resume compaction\n\n5. **Manual Block Truncation (Last Resort)**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove partial/temporary blocks:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n6. **Monitor Progress**\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` for changes\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increasing\n   - Verify `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` returns to 0\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction loop: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compact method: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n- Block write with timeout: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Context cancellation: compaction respects context cancellation (tsdb/db.go:830, 941)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus fails to start with errors like:\n  ```\n  msg=\"failed to reload blocks\" err=\"validate block: invalid meta.json: version mismatch\"\n  msg=\"corruption detected in block\" ulid=<ULID>\n  ```\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Some queries fail with \"series not found\" or \"chunk corrupted\"\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` drops unexpectedly\n- WAL reader corruption errors in logs\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Disk corruption** (bit flip, partial write on power loss)\n- **Abrupt process termination** during block write (SIGKILL, OOM kill)\n- **Filesystem issues** (full disk during write, corrupted inode)\n- **Migration errors** (blocks moved between systems without verification)\n- **Concurrent block modification** (multiple Prometheus instances on same TSDB)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check block metadata:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n   Look for blocks with errors in validation.\n\n2. Identify corrupted block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path 2>&1 | grep -i \"error\\|invalid\"\n   ```\n\n3. Dump block to verify:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> --max-time=<ts> | head -20\n   ```\n   If samples can't be decoded, block is corrupt.\n\n4. Check filesystem:\n   ```bash\n   fsck /dev/xxx  # Unmount first!\n   smartctl -a /dev/xxx  # Check disk health\n   ```\n\n5. Verify meta.json of suspect block:\n   ```bash\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>/meta.json | jq .\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Isolate Corruption**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Identify corrupted block ULID from logs\n\n2. **Backup (Before Deletion)**\n   ```bash\n   tar czf corrupted-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete Corrupted Block**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Remove Temporary/Partial Blocks**\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n5. **Attempt Repair (If Meta Intact)**\n   - If only chunk/index corrupted, promtool can sometimes repair:\n     ```bash\n     # Check if repairable\n     promtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n     ```\n\n6. **Restart and Rebuild**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   # Monitor logs for re-replay of WAL\n   tail -f prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n7. **Data Recovery**\n   - **If using remote storage**: Enable remote read to restore missing data\n   - **If high availability**: Resync from backup/standby Prometheus\n   - **Otherwise**: Data in deleted block is permanently lost (retention tradeoff)\n\n8. **Prevent Recurrence**\n   - Enable filesystem checksums (ZFS, BTRFS recommended)\n   - Add monitoring for disk errors: `smartctl -x /dev/xxx`\n   - Ensure UPS for stable power\n   - Distribute TSDB across multiple filesystems\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Block validation: `block.go` meta validation functions\n- Corruption detection: `OpenBlock()` (tsdb/block.go)\n- Repair tool: `cmd/promtool/tsdb.go repair command`\n- Meta file reading: `readMetaFile()` (tsdb/block.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction process killed with: `Killed` or `SIGKILL` (often from Linux OOM killer)\n- Prometheus restart logs show: `signal: killed` or `memory exceeded`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1, then reset after restart\n- System memory usage spikes during compaction, then crashes\n- Partial/corrupted blocks appear: `*.tmp-for-creation` files remain\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Insufficient memory for block write** (default 512MB chunk segment size)\n- **Cardinality explosion** (millions of series in single block)\n- **Memory leak** in compaction logic (less likely but possible in edge cases)\n- **Container/systemd memory limit** set too low\n- **Other processes competing** for memory\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check memory during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n   # Watch RSS (resident set size)\n   ```\n\n2. Check system memory:\n   ```bash\n   free -h\n   top -b -n 1 | head -20\n   ```\n\n3. Check cgroup/container limits:\n   ```bash\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes  # In bytes\n   grep memory /proc/<prometheus-pid>/cgroup\n   ```\n\n4. Check block sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable | tail -10\n   # Look for very large blocks (>5GB)\n   ```\n\n5. Check series cardinality in largest block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> | wc -l\n   ```\n\n6. Review Prometheus logs for memory pressure:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"memory\\|oom\\|killed\" prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Mitigation**\n   - Increase available memory (VM: add RAM; Container: increase limit)\n   - OR reduce memory footprint:\n\n2. **Reduce Memory Footprint**\n\n   **Option A: Increase `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size`**\n   - Default: 512MB (compaction buffers data before writing segments)\n   - Increase to 1GB or 2GB to reduce number of segment writes:\n     ```\n     --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=2147483648  # 2GB\n     ```\n\n   **Option B: Reduce Ingestion Rate**\n   - Temporarily disable or throttle scrape jobs\n   - Reduce cardinality (relabel_drop high-cardinality labels)\n\n   **Option C: Reduce Retention**\n   - Reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `.size`\n   - Forces more aggressive block deletion\n\n3. **Clean Up Partial Blocks**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove incomplete compactions:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -delete\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -delete\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n4. **Restart with New Configuration**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # Update /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml or systemd unit\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor Next Compaction Cycle**\n   - Watch memory usage during compaction:\n     ```\n     max(process_resident_memory_bytes)\n     ```\n   - Should stay below 70% of available memory\n   - If still failing, more aggressive mitigation needed\n\n6. **Long-term Solution**\n   - Add more RAM to the system\n   - Split TSDB into multiple instances with federation\n   - Use remote storage to reduce on-disk blocks\n   - Implement better cardinality management (label relabeling, dropping)\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Memory allocation during block write: `PopulateBlock()` (tsdb/compact.go:729-874)\n- Chunk segment writing: `chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize()` (tsdb/chunks/chunks.go)\n- Process memory metric: `process_resident_memory_bytes` (Go runtime metrics)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### General Recovery Decision Tree\n\n```\nSymptom: Compaction issues detected\n│\n├─ Disk space error?\n│  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 1 (Disk Space Exhaustion)\n│\n├─ Compaction stuck (>10 min)?\n│  ├─ OOM in logs?\n│  │  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 4 (OOM)\n│  ├─ Disk I/O saturated?\n│  │  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 2 step \"Disk I/O Bottleneck\"\n│  └─ Other?\n│     └─ Follow: Failure Mode 2 (Compaction Stuck)\n│\n├─ Block errors during startup?\n│  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 3 (Block Corruption)\n│\n└─ Compaction running but slow?\n   ├─ Duration increasing?\n   │  └─ Likely approaching disk/memory limits, follow Mode 1 or 4\n   └─ Check metrics for anomalies (Mode 2 diagnostic steps)\n```\n\n### Emergency Shutdown & Recovery\n\n**When to use**: Compaction completely broken, Prometheus unstable, immediate action needed.\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# Emergency recovery script\n\nTSDB_PATH=\"/var/lib/prometheus\"\nBACKUP_DIR=\"/var/backups/prometheus-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\"\n\n# 1. Shutdown Prometheus\necho \"[1] Stopping Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl stop prometheus || kill -TERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 10\nkill -9 $(pgrep prometheus) 2>/dev/null || true\n\n# 2. Backup current state\necho \"[2] Backing up TSDB...\"\nmkdir -p \"$BACKUP_DIR\"\ntar czf \"$BACKUP_DIR/tsdb-backup.tar.gz\" \"$TSDB_PATH\" 2>&1 | tail -5\n\n# 3. Clean temporary blocks\necho \"[3] Cleaning temporary blocks...\"\nfind \"$TSDB_PATH\" -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rfv {} \\; 2>&1 | wc -l\n\n# 4. Inspect blocks\necho \"[4] Analyzing blocks...\"\npromtool tsdb list \"$TSDB_PATH\" --human-readable | tail -20\n\n# 5. Identify and isolate issues\necho \"[5] Checking for corruption...\"\nfor block in \"$TSDB_PATH\"/*; do\n  if [[ -d \"$block\" && ! \"$block\" =~ wal$ ]]; then\n    if ! promtool tsdb inspect \"$block\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n      echo \"CORRUPTED: $block\"\n      mv \"$block\" \"$block.corrupted\"\n    fi\n  fi\ndone\n\n# 6. Restart\necho \"[6] Restarting Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl start prometheus\nsleep 5\n\n# 7. Verify\necho \"[7] Verification...\"\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\necho \"\"\ntail -20 /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n```\n\n### Using promtool for Inspection & Recovery\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with human-readable output\npromtool tsdb list /var/lib/prometheus --human-readable\n\n# Analyze compaction efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /var/lib/prometheus\n\n# Dump specific time range (for audit)\npromtool tsdb dump /var/lib/prometheus \\\n  --min-time=1609459200000 \\\n  --max-time=1609545600000 \\\n  --match='{job=\"prometheus\"}' > dump.txt\n\n# Verify block integrity\npromtool tsdb inspect /var/lib/prometheus/<ULID>\n\n# (Attempted) Repair corrupted blocks\npromtool tsdb repair /var/lib/prometheus\n```\n\n### Preventing Future Compaction Issues\n\n**Monitoring & Alerting:**\n\n```yaml\n# Prometheus alert rule example\ngroups:\n  - name: tsdb_compaction\n    rules:\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionsFailing\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compactions failing\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionStuck\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n          and changes(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[10m]) == 0\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction stuck for 10+ minutes\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBDiskSpaceRunningOut\n        expr: (prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes) > 0.85\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus disk usage > 85% of retention limit\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionTakingTooLong\n        expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds) > 7200\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus p99 compaction duration > 2 hours (block range)\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBBlocksHighCardinality\n        expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total[5m]) > 0.1\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"High rate of vertical (overlapping) compactions\"\n```\n\n**Operational Best Practices:**\n\n1. **Retention Configuration**\n   - Size: Set `storage.tsdb.retention.size` to 80% of available disk\n   - Time: Balance query SLA (query_max_time) with storage costs\n   - Example: `retention.time=30d retention.size=500GB`\n\n2. **Resource Allocation**\n   - Memory: Allocate 2-4GB minimum; large cardinality may need 8-16GB\n   - CPU: Dedicate 2-4 cores to Prometheus; compaction uses all available\n   - Disk: Use SSDs; HDD I/O is major bottleneck\n\n3. **Cardinality Management**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes`\n   - Use relabeling to drop high-cardinality labels\n   - Example: drop `pod_id`, `container_id` if not needed\n\n4. **High Availability**\n   - Run multiple Prometheus instances with remote storage\n   - Use WAL in remote storage for durability\n   - Federation for aggregation without compaction contention\n\n5. **Scheduled Maintenance**\n   - Weekly: `promtool tsdb analyze` for efficiency report\n   - Monthly: verify block checksums, backup critical blocks\n   - Quarterly: review retention policy based on query patterns\n\n---\n\n## 5. tsdb/compact.go:107 | Gauge | Set 1 at line 748, 0 at line 746 |\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Quick Reference\n\n### Command Cheat Sheet\n\n```bash\n# Check TSDB health\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus --human-readable\n\n# Analyze blocks\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus\n\n# Inspect specific block\npromtool tsdb inspect /path/to/prometheus/<ULID>\n\n# Dump samples for verification\npromtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus --min-time=<ts> --max-time=<ts>\n\n# Repair (use with caution)\npromtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus\n\n# Flush WAL to blocks (read-only mode)\npromtool query tsdb flushwal /path/to/prometheus\n\n# Check Prometheus via API\ncurl http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\ncurl http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep tsdb_compaction\n\n# Force clean tombstones via API\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/clean_tombstones\n```\n\n### Configuration Reference\n\n```yaml\n# prometheus.yml relevant sections\nglobal:\n max 500GB (whichever first)\n    max_block_chunk_segment_size: 536870912  # 512MB (default)\n\n# Command-line equivalent\n# --storage.tsdb.path=/var/lib/prometheus\n# --storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d\n# --storage.tsdb.retention.size=500GB\n# --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=536870912\n```\n\n### Sample Metric Queries\n\n```promql\n# Compaction frequency\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[5m])\n\n# Failed compactions\nincrease(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h])\n\n# Compaction duration (p99)\nhistogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds)\n\n# Block count\nprometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n\n# Storage usage\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / 1e9  # In GB\n\n# Memory usage\nprocess_resident_memory_bytes / 1e9  # In GB\n\n# Disk saturation\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nTSDB compaction is a critical background process for maintaining query performance and disk space efficiency. The key to operational stability is:\n\n1. **Monitor** compaction metrics continuously (failure count, duration, block count)\n2. **Alert** on anomalies (stuck compactions, failures, disk saturation)\n3. **Size** resources appropriately (memory, disk, CPU)\n4. **Plan** retention carefully (balance query window vs. storage cost)\n5. **Act quickly** when issues arise (recovery procedures in this runbook)\n\nMost issues can be prevented through proper sizing and monitoring. When incidents do occur, this runbook provides diagnostic procedures and recovery steps for rapid resolution.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":12428,"cache_read_input_tokens":83988,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":12428},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"700510f8-a464-4312-9b9d-2ac5689d1c25","uuid":"365ed086-9cd4-46ab-b455-85501e8eac78"}

Overview\n\n### What is Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time-series blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. It serves three primary purposes:\n\n1. **Space Efficiency**: Consolidates data from smaller 2-hour blocks into larger blocks (up to 31 days or 10% of retention), reducing metadata overhead\n2. **Query Performance**: Fewer blocks to scan during queries, reducing I/O and improving query speed\n3. **Tombstone Cleanup**: Removes series marked for deletion (via tombstones), recovering disk space\n\n### Block Structure\n\nPrometheus stores time-series data in a hierarchical block structure with exponential block durations:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: In-memory head block, ~2 hours of data\n- **Level 1-10**: Persisted blocks with exponentially increasing durations\n  - Each level is ~3x larger than the previous level\n  - Example: 2h → 6h → 18h → 54h → ... → 31 days\n  - Blocks containing tombstones (>5% deleted series) are also compacted\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered through two mechanisms:\n\n| Trigger Type | Frequency | Condition |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Head Block Compaction** | On append commit | `head.compactable()` returns true when head block age > `chunkRange / 2` |\n| **Scheduled Compaction** | Every 1 minute | Regular background loop in `db.run()` checks for blocks ready to compact |\n| **Block Compaction** | On-demand | Multiple level-0/1 blocks fitting within a time range are merged upward |\n\n**Code References:**\n- Head compaction trigger: `dbAppender.Commit()` (tsdb/db.go:1115-1127)\n- Scheduled trigger: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compaction logic: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Critical Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Execution Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Increasing | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions scheduled | Increasing regularly | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compaction attempts | Should be 0 or growing slowly | `increase(...[1h]) > 5` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to auto-compact disabled | Stable or low | `rate(...[5m]) > 0` indicates disabled compaction |\n\n#### Performance Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` (histogram) | Histogram | Time to complete compaction | p99 < block_duration | p99 > `chunkRange` (2h default) suggests falling behind |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` (gauge) | Gauge | Block being written (1=yes, 0=no) | 0 (not perpetually writing) | Stuck at 1 for >10 minutes |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases as blocks overlap | Rapid increase suggests ingestion delays |\n\n#### Block & Storage Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of persistent blocks in memory | Increases then stable | Continuously increasing suggests compaction not running |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` | Gauge | Memory for symbol tables across blocks | Stable/growing slowly | Rapid growth with `blocks_loaded` suggests memory leak |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Disk space used by blocks | Stable near `retention_limit_bytes` | Exceeds `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max retention size | Set once | Mismatch with actual disk usage |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (time-based) | Stable or increasing | Increasing rapidly suggests retention misconfiguration |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (size-based) | Stable or slow increase | Increasing suggests `MaxBytes` limit being hit |\n\n#### WAL/Checkpointing Metrics\n\n| Metric | Meaning | Healthy | Watch For |\n|--------|---------|---------|-----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total` | WAL corruption count | 0 or stable | Increasing indicates disk issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_truncate_duration_seconds` | WAL truncation time | < 1 second | > 5 seconds suggests slow disk I/O |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Indicators\n\nA healthy Prometheus instance should exhibit:\n\n```\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total continuously increasing\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total stable (not growing)\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 < 2 hours (default block range)\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded stable after reaching equilibrium\n✓ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 0 (not perpetually writing)\n✓ No increase in prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total\n```\n\n### Stuck Compaction Indicators\n\nCompaction is stuck if:\n\n```\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 1 for >10 minutes\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 > 2× block_duration\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded continuously increasing\n✗ prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total increasing but compactions_failed_total also increasing\n✗ Logs show \"compaction failed\" repeatedly\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` exceeds available disk space\n- Compaction fails with I/O errors\n- Prometheus logs: `error: write block: no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New samples may be rejected; WAL may grow unbounded\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Retention period/MaxBytes configured too large for available disk\n- Compaction not running (blocks accumulate uncompacted)\n- Retention deletion running slower than ingestion\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage and free space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect block count and sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n3. Check Prometheus metrics:\n   ```\n   prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes (current size)\n   prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes (configured limit)\n   prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded (number of blocks)\n   ```\n\n4. Review Prometheus logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compaction\\|disk\\|space\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Action (Buy Time)**\n   - Stop ingestion temporarily (pause scrape jobs) if possible\n   - Disable auto-compaction to free CPU for deletion:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n2. **Free Disk Space (Choose One)**\n\n   **Option A: Reduce Retention**\n   - Edit `prometheus.yml`, reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `storage.tsdb.retention.size`\n   - Restart Prometheus\n   - Blocks older than new retention are deleted on next compaction\n\n   **Option B: Manual Block Deletion**\n   - **Backup first**: `tar czf prometheus-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/blocks/`\n   - List blocks by age:\n     ```bash\n     promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable\n     ```\n   - Manually delete oldest blocks (oldest ULID = earliest blocks):\n     ```bash\n     rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/01ARZ3NHH000000000 # Replace ULID\n     ```\n   - Reload Prometheus via admin API:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n   **Option C: Extend Disk (Preferred Long-term)**\n   - Add more disk capacity\n   - Mount at same path or symlink\n\n3. **Restart Compaction**\n   ```bash\n   # Enable auto-compaction (if disabled)\n   curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/clean_tombstones\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify Recovery**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` decreasing\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` stops increasing\n   - Re-enable scrape jobs\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction error handling: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Retention deletion: `db.reloadBlocks()` (tsdb/db.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 10 minutes (stuck at \"writing block\")\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` histogram not updating\n- Prometheus CPU usage high, disk I/O high, but no new blocks created\n- Logs show \"compact blocks\" but no completion\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Out-of-Memory (OOM) killing compaction process** (see Failure Mode 4)\n- **Disk I/O bottleneck** (slow SSDs, network storage, VM I/O throttling)\n- **Lock contention** (cmtx held, blocking other operations)\n- **Query load during compaction** interfering with I/O scheduling\n- **WAL replay still running** in background, holding file locks\n- **Context cancelled** (Prometheus shutting down, compaction context timed out)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check compaction duration trend:\n   ```\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_sum[5m]) / rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_count[5m])\n   ```\n   Should complete in < 2 hours (default block duration)\n\n2. Check if block is being written:\n   ```bash\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n   ```\n   If true for > 10 min, compaction is stuck.\n\n3. Check for hanging processes:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus  # Check CPU/memory\n   lsof /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path | head -20  # Check open files\n   ```\n\n4. Check disk I/O:\n   ```bash\n   iostat -x 1 10  # Check %utilization, await time\n   iotop -o        # Monitor top I/O processes\n   ```\n\n5. Review recent logs:\n   ```bash\n   tail -100 prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|error\\|warn\"\n   ```\n\n6. Check WAL replay status:\n   ```\n   # Look for \"msg\"=\"WAL read\" or \"OOO replay\" in logs\n   grep -i \"wal read\\|ooo.*replay\" prometheus.log | tail -10\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Determine Root Cause** (from diagnostics above)\n\n2. **If OOM (see Failure Mode 4)**\n   - Increase memory limit\n   - Reduce `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size` (default 512MB)\n   - Reduce ingestion rate\n\n3. **If Disk I/O Bottleneck**\n   - Reduce query concurrency (scale down dashboards/alerts)\n   - Move TSDB to faster storage (SSD preferred)\n   - For network storage: check latency, throughput, cache settings\n\n4. **If Compaction Truly Stuck (20+ minutes)**\n   - Stop Prometheus gracefully:\n     ```bash\n     kill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n     # Wait up to 5 minutes for graceful shutdown\n     sleep 300\n     kill -9 <prometheus-pid>  # Force if needed\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus:\n     ```bash\n     systemctl restart prometheus\n     # OR\n     /path/to/prometheus --config.file=prometheus.yml\n     ```\n   - Prometheus will replay WAL and resume compaction\n\n5. **Manual Block Truncation (Last Resort)**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove partial/temporary blocks:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n6. **Monitor Progress**\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` for changes\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increasing\n   - Verify `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` returns to 0\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction loop: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compact method: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n- Block write with timeout: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Context cancellation: compaction respects context cancellation (tsdb/db.go:830, 941)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus fails to start with errors like:\n  ```\n  msg=\"failed to reload blocks\" err=\"validate block: invalid meta.json: version mismatch\"\n  msg=\"corruption detected in block\" ulid=<ULID>\n  ```\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Some queries fail with \"series not found\" or \"chunk corrupted\"\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` drops unexpectedly\n- WAL reader corruption errors in logs\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Disk corruption** (bit flip, partial write on power loss)\n- **Abrupt process termination** during block write (SIGKILL, OOM kill)\n- **Filesystem issues** (full disk during write, corrupted inode)\n- **Migration errors** (blocks moved between systems without verification)\n- **Concurrent block modification** (multiple Prometheus instances on same TSDB)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check block metadata:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n   Look for blocks with errors in validation.\n\n2. Identify corrupted block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path 2>&1 | grep -i \"error\\|invalid\"\n   ```\n\n3. Dump block to verify:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> --max-time=<ts> | head -20\n   ```\n   If samples can't be decoded, block is corrupt.\n\n4. Check filesystem:\n   ```bash\n   fsck /dev/xxx  # Unmount first!\n   smartctl -a /dev/xxx  # Check disk health\n   ```\n\n5. Verify meta.json of suspect block:\n   ```bash\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>/meta.json | jq .\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Isolate Corruption**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Identify corrupted block ULID from logs\n\n2. **Backup (Before Deletion)**\n   ```bash\n   tar czf corrupted-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete Corrupted Block**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Remove Temporary/Partial Blocks**\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n5. **Attempt Repair (If Meta Intact)**\n   - If only chunk/index corrupted, promtool can sometimes repair:\n     ```bash\n     # Check if repairable\n     promtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n     ```\n\n6. **Restart and Rebuild**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   # Monitor logs for re-replay of WAL\n   tail -f prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n7. **Data Recovery**\n   - **If using remote storage**: Enable remote read to restore missing data\n   - **If high availability**: Resync from backup/standby Prometheus\n   - **Otherwise**: Data in deleted block is permanently lost (retention tradeoff)\n\n8. **Prevent Recurrence**\n   - Enable filesystem checksums (ZFS, BTRFS recommended)\n   - Add monitoring for disk errors: `smartctl -x /dev/xxx`\n   - Ensure UPS for stable power\n   - Distribute TSDB across multiple filesystems\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Block validation: `block.go` meta validation functions\n- Corruption detection: `OpenBlock()` (tsdb/block.go)\n- Repair tool: `cmd/promtool/tsdb.go repair command`\n- Meta file reading: `readMetaFile()` (tsdb/block.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction process killed with: `Killed` or `SIGKILL` (often from Linux OOM killer)\n- Prometheus restart logs show: `signal: killed` or `memory exceeded`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1, then reset after restart\n- System memory usage spikes during compaction, then crashes\n- Partial/corrupted blocks appear: `*.tmp-for-creation` files remain\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Insufficient memory for block write** (default 512MB chunk segment size)\n- **Cardinality explosion** (millions of series in single block)\n- **Memory leak** in compaction logic (less likely but possible in edge cases)\n- **Container/systemd memory limit** set too low\n- **Other processes competing** for memory\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check memory during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n   # Watch RSS (resident set size)\n   ```\n\n2. Check system memory:\n   ```bash\n   free -h\n   top -b -n 1 | head -20\n   ```\n\n3. Check cgroup/container limits:\n   ```bash\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes  # In bytes\n   grep memory /proc/<prometheus-pid>/cgroup\n   ```\n\n4. Check block sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable | tail -10\n   # Look for very large blocks (>5GB)\n   ```\n\n5. Check series cardinality in largest block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> | wc -l\n   ```\n\n6. Review Prometheus logs for memory pressure:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"memory\\|oom\\|killed\" prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Mitigation**\n   - Increase available memory (VM: add RAM; Container: increase limit)\n   - OR reduce memory footprint:\n\n2. **Reduce Memory Footprint**\n\n   **Option A: Increase `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size`**\n   - Default: 512MB (compaction buffers data before writing segments)\n   - Increase to 1GB or 2GB to reduce number of segment writes:\n     ```\n     --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=2147483648  # 2GB\n     ```\n\n   **Option B: Reduce Ingestion Rate**\n   - Temporarily disable or throttle scrape jobs\n   - Reduce cardinality (relabel_drop high-cardinality labels)\n\n   **Option C: Reduce Retention**\n   - Reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `.size`\n   - Forces more aggressive block deletion\n\n3. **Clean Up Partial Blocks**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove incomplete compactions:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -delete\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -delete\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n4. **Restart with New Configuration**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # Update /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml or systemd unit\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor Next Compaction Cycle**\n   - Watch memory usage during compaction:\n     ```\n     max(process_resident_memory_bytes)\n     ```\n   - Should stay below 70% of available memory\n   - If still failing, more aggressive mitigation needed\n\n6. **Long-term Solution**\n   - Add more RAM to the system\n   - Split TSDB into multiple instances with federation\n   - Use remote storage to reduce on-disk blocks\n   - Implement better cardinality management (label relabeling, dropping)\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Memory allocation during block write: `PopulateBlock()` (tsdb/compact.go:729-874)\n- Chunk segment writing: `chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize()` (tsdb/chunks/chunks.go)\n- Process memory metric: `process_resident_memory_bytes` (Go runtime metrics)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### General Recovery Decision Tree\n\n```\nSymptom: Compaction issues detected\n│\n├─ Disk space error?\n│  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 1 (Disk Space Exhaustion)\n│\n├─ Compaction stuck (>10 min)?\n│  ├─ OOM in logs?\n│  │  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 4 (OOM)\n│  ├─ Disk I/O saturated?\n│  │  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 2 step \"Disk I/O Bottleneck\"\n│  └─ Other?\n│     └─ Follow: Failure Mode 2 (Compaction Stuck)\n│\n├─ Block errors during startup?\n│  └─ Follow: Failure Mode 3 (Block Corruption)\n│\n└─ Compaction running but slow?\n   ├─ Duration increasing?\n   │  └─ Likely approaching disk/memory limits, follow Mode 1 or 4\n   └─ Check metrics for anomalies (Mode 2 diagnostic steps)\n```\n\n### Emergency Shutdown & Recovery\n\n**When to use**: Compaction completely broken, Prometheus unstable, immediate action needed.\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# Emergency recovery script\n\nTSDB_PATH=\"/var/lib/prometheus\"\nBACKUP_DIR=\"/var/backups/prometheus-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\"\n\n# 1. Shutdown Prometheus\necho \"[1] Stopping Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl stop prometheus || kill -TERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 10\nkill -9 $(pgrep prometheus) 2>/dev/null || true\n\n# 2. Backup current state\necho \"[2] Backing up TSDB...\"\nmkdir -p \"$BACKUP_DIR\"\ntar czf \"$BACKUP_DIR/tsdb-backup.tar.gz\" \"$TSDB_PATH\" 2>&1 | tail -5\n\n# 3. Clean temporary blocks\necho \"[3] Cleaning temporary blocks...\"\nfind \"$TSDB_PATH\" -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rfv {} \\; 2>&1 | wc -l\n\n# 4. Inspect blocks\necho \"[4] Analyzing blocks...\"\npromtool tsdb list \"$TSDB_PATH\" --human-readable | tail -20\n\n# 5. Identify and isolate issues\necho \"[5] Checking for corruption...\"\nfor block in \"$TSDB_PATH\"/*; do\n  if [[ -d \"$block\" && ! \"$block\" =~ wal$ ]]; then\n    if ! promtool tsdb inspect \"$block\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n      echo \"CORRUPTED: $block\"\n      mv \"$block\" \"$block.corrupted\"\n    fi\n  fi\ndone\n\n# 6. Restart\necho \"[6] Restarting Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl start prometheus\nsleep 5\n\n# 7. Verify\necho \"[7] Verification...\"\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\necho \"\"\ntail -20 /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n```\n\n### Using promtool for Inspection & Recovery\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with human-readable output\npromtool tsdb list /var/lib/prometheus --human-readable\n\n# Analyze compaction efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /var/lib/prometheus\n\n# Dump specific time range (for audit)\npromtool tsdb dump /var/lib/prometheus \\\n  --min-time=1609459200000 \\\n  --max-time=1609545600000 \\\n  --match='{job=\"prometheus\"}' > dump.txt\n\n# Verify block integrity\npromtool tsdb inspect /var/lib/prometheus/<ULID>\n\n# (Attempted) Repair corrupted blocks\npromtool tsdb repair /var/lib/prometheus\n```\n\n### Preventing Future Compaction Issues\n\n**Monitoring & Alerting:**\n\n```yaml\n# Prometheus alert rule example\ngroups:\n  - name: tsdb_compaction\n    rules:\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionsFailing\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compactions failing\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionStuck\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n          and changes(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[10m]) == 0\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction stuck for 10+ minutes\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBDiskSpaceRunningOut\n        expr: (prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes) > 0.85\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus disk usage > 85% of retention limit\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionTakingTooLong\n        expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds) > 7200\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus p99 compaction duration > 2 hours (block range)\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBBlocksHighCardinality\n        expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total[5m]) > 0.1\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"High rate of vertical (overlapping) compactions\"\n```\n\n**Operational Best Practices:**\n\n1. **Retention Configuration**\n   - Size: Set `storage.tsdb.retention.size` to 80% of available disk\n   - Time: Balance query SLA (query_max_time) with storage costs\n   - Example: `retention.time=30d retention.size=500GB`\n\n2. **Resource Allocation**\n   - Memory: Allocate 2-4GB minimum; large cardinality may need 8-16GB\n   - CPU: Dedicate 2-4 cores to Prometheus; compaction uses all available\n   - Disk: Use SSDs; HDD I/O is major bottleneck\n\n3. **Cardinality Management**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes`\n   - Use relabeling to drop high-cardinality labels\n   - Example: drop `pod_id`, `container_id` if not needed\n\n4. **High Availability**\n   - Run multiple Prometheus instances with remote storage\n   - Use WAL in remote storage for durability\n   - Federation for aggregation without compaction contention\n\n5. **Scheduled Maintenance**\n   - Weekly: `promtool tsdb analyze` for efficiency report\n   - Monthly: verify block checksums, backup critical blocks\n   - Quarterly: review retention policy based on query patterns\n\n---\n\n## 5.
